[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         A critical security vulnerability has been detected during fuzzing of the Apache    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Tika CLI component. The issue is a file path traversal vulnerability that allows an [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         attacker to write files outside of the intended directory by using relative path    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         sequences [1m([0m..[35m/[0m[1m)[0m in file paths. The vulnerability was triggered when processing an   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         embedded document during package parsing, where the path                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[35m/tmp/expander-tmp15896470530042338828/output/q/r/s/t/../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m` was   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         flagged as a security violation.                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The issue manifests as a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception thrown by the      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Jazzer fuzzer's file path traversal sanitizer. The exception indicates that a file  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         path traversal attempt was detected during the extraction of embedded documents     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         from a package archive.                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Vulnerability Type                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         This is a **file path traversal vulnerability** [1m([0malso known as directory traversal  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         or path traversal[1m)[0m, a critical security issue that can allow an attacker to access  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         or write files in locations outside of the intended directory structure.            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Important Observations                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. **Attack Vector**: The vulnerability occurs during the unpacking/extraction      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         process when Tika processes package files containing embedded documents. The        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         malicious path `q/r/s/t/..[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m` demonstrates how relative path      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         sequences can be used to escape the intended output directory structure.            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. **Call Chain Analysis**: The vulnerability is triggered through the following    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         execution path:                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - `[1;35mTikaCLI.main[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` → Entry point for CLI processing                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - `[1;35mTikaCLI.process[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` → Main processing logic                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - `[1;35mOutputType.process[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` → Handles output processing                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - `[1;35mAutoDetectParser.parse[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` → Automatic format detection and parsing            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - `[1;35mPackageParser.parse[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` → Package file parsing                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - `[1;35mPackageParser._parse[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` → Internal parsing implementation                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - `[1;35mPackageParser.parseEntries[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` → Iterates through package entries              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - `[1;35mPackageParser.parseEntry[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` → Processes individual entries                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - `[1;35mFileEmbeddedDocumentExtractor.parseEmbedded[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` → **Critical point where file  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         path is constructed and used**                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. **Affected Component**: The primary component involved is                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `TikaCLI.FileEmbeddedDocumentExtractor` at line [1;36m1111[0m, which is responsible for      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         extracting embedded documents from packages. This component appears to use file     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         paths from the package entries without proper sanitization.                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. **Temporary Directory Usage**: The output directory is a temporary location      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0m`[35m/tmp/expander-tmp15896470530042338828/output/[0m`[1m)[0m, suggesting this occurs during    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         temporary file extraction operations.                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Areas for Investigation                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         To fully understand and address this vulnerability, the following components should [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         be thoroughly investigated:                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. **`org.apache.tika.cli.TikaCLI.FileEmbeddedDocumentExtractor`** [1m([0mline [1;36m1111[0m[1m)[0m:     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Examine how this class constructs file paths when extracting embedded documents and [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         whether it performs any path validation or sanitization.                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. **`org.apache.tika.parser.pkg.PackageParser`**: Review the `[1;35mparseEntry[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` method [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0mline [1;36m481[0m[1m)[0m and related methods to understand how entry names/paths are extracted    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         from package archives and passed to the document extractor.                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. **Path Construction Logic**: Identify where and how file paths are constructed   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         when creating output files for extracted content. Determine if paths from untrusted [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         package entries are directly used without normalization.                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. **Output Directory Management**: Investigate how the output directory is         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         established and whether there are any existing boundary checks to prevent files     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         from being written outside this directory.                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m. **Entry Name Handling**: Examine how entry names are retrieved from various      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         package formats [1m([0mZIP, TAR, etc.[1m)[0m and whether different package parsers have         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         consistent handling of path traversal sequences.                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m. **Configuration Options**: Check if there are any CLI options or configuration   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         settings related to path handling, output directories, or security restrictions     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         that may be relevant to this issue.                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m102[0m[39m:        int unix = [0m[1;35mpath.lastIndexOf[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"/"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis of the Vulnerability[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the code snippets and evaluation report, I've identified the root [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause of the file path traversal vulnerability:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Entry Point**: The vulnerability occurs in [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mTikaCLI.FileEmbeddedDocumentExtractor.getOutputFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1128[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1169[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Attack Flow**:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Malicious archive contains entry with path traversal: [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`q/r/s/t/..[0m[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - PackageParser extracts entry name without sanitization [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m444[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Entry name stored in metadata as `TikaCoreProperties.RESOURCE_NAME_KEY` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m223[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - TikaCLI's FileEmbeddedDocumentExtractor receives this in `[0m[1;35mparseEmbedded[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1095[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mgetOutputFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` attempts normalization using Apache Commons IO [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mFilenameUtils.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1141[0m[1;39m)[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - BUT: Apache Commons IO's `[0m[1;35mnormalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` doesn't prevent path traversal when the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresult is used with `File` constructor[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mextractDir, normalizedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m1160[0m[39m creates a File object that[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcan escape extractDir[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No validation that the final `outputFile` is within `extractDir` before [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwriting [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1111[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Why Current Code Fails**:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Uses wrong `FilenameUtils` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mApache Commons IO instead of Tika's own[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Apache Commons IO's `[0m[1;35mnormalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` resolves [0m[32m".."[0m[39m but doesn't prevent the result[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom escaping parent when used with File constructor[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Missing canonical path validation like the pattern used in `FileSystemFetcher`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m78[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m82[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Tika's Own Documentation Warns About This**:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35morg.apache.tika.io.FilenameUtils.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` javadoc [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m84[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m90[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m explicitly [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwarns: [0m[32m"If a careless client used that filename as if it were a filename and not a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mpath when writing embedded files, bad things could happen. Consider: [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m'../../../my_ppt.ppt'."[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix Location: `tika-app/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/cli/TikaCLI.java`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Modify the `[0m[1;35mFileEmbeddedDocumentExtractor.getOutputFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1128[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1169[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Change the import and sanitization approach**:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep the Apache Commons IO import but supplement with Tika's own FilenameUtils[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After line [0m[1;36m59[0m[39m, ensure Tika's FilenameUtils can be accessed [0m[1;39m([0m[39mit's in tika-core [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdependency[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Update the `[0m[1;35mgetOutputFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method logic**:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m **Use Tika's [0m[1;35mFilenameUtils.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for initial sanitization** [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1141[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Replace or supplement the Apache Commons IO [0m[1;35mnormalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with Tika's [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Tika's [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m extracts ONLY the filename, removing all directory path [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomponents[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This prevents path traversal by design[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Keep the null byte replacement [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1140[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Apply Tika's [0m[1;35mnormalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m after [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to handle reserved characters[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m **Add canonical path validation** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m1160[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - After constructing `outputFile`, validate it's within `extractDir`[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Use the pattern from FileSystemFetcher: check that the canonical/real path [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstarts with extractDir's canonical/real path[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Throw an IOException if validation fails[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This provides defense-in-depth even if [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m has edge cases[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Specific implementation steps**:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m**: Around line [0m[1;36m1141[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1154[0m[39m, replace the normalization logic:[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Current logic uses:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Apache Commons IO [0m[1;35mFilenameUtils.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Then falls back to [0m[1;35mFilenameUtils.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m if normalize returns null[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Then strips prefix[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     New logic should:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - First use Tika's [0m[1;35mFilenameUtils.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to extract just the filename [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mremoves all path components[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Then apply Tika's [0m[1;35mFilenameUtils.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to handle reserved characters[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - This completely removes the path traversal attack vector[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m**: After line [0m[1;36m1160[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter `File outputFile = new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mextractDir, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalizedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add validation:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Validate that outputFile is within extractDir:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Get canonical paths of both outputFile and extractDir[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Check that outputFile's canonical path starts with extractDir's canonical [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Throw IOException with descriptive message if validation fails[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Handle the case where outputFile doesn't exist yet [0m[1;39m([0m[39muse [0m[1;35mgetCanonicalFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor [0m[1;35mgetAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m**: For the duplicate file handling [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1162[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1167[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, apply the same [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation after creating the UUID-prefixed file[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Preserve existing functionality**:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep extension handling [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1129[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1132[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep relationship ID prefixing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1134[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1137[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep URL decoding [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1155[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1159[0m[1;39m)[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep duplicate file handling with UUID [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1162[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1167[0m[1;39m)[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep parent directory creation logic in [0m[1;35mparseEmbedded[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1103[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1108[0m[1;39m)[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Approach is Optimal[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Defense in Depth**: Uses two layers of protection:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - First layer: Remove path components entirely with Tika's [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Second layer: Validate canonical path as safety net[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Follows Tika's Own Guidelines**: The javadoc for Tika's [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFilenameUtils.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m explicitly recommends this approach for security[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Consistent with Existing Patterns**: FileSystemFetcher already uses canonical [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m78[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m82[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so this makes the codebase consistent[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Minimal Disruption**: Only modifies the vulnerable method, doesn't change APIs[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor break existing tests[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Comprehensive Protection**: Handles all path traversal techniques:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Relative paths with [0m[32m".."[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[32m"../../evil.txt"[0m[1;39m)[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Deeply nested traversals [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[32m"q/r/s/t/../../jazzer-traversal"[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Absolute paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39malready handled by prefix stripping, but validated by [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcanonical check[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Symbolic links [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhandled by canonical path resolution[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Impact on Existing Logic[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Files will be extracted with only their filename** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnot full paths[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Before: [0m[32m"dir1/dir2/file.txt"[0m[39m → extracts to [0m[32m"extractDir/dir1/dir2/file.txt"[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After: [0m[32m"dir1/dir2/file.txt"[0m[39m → extracts to [0m[32m"extractDir/file.txt"[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This is actually SAFER and more expected behavior for archive extraction[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Subdirectories from archives won't be preserved, but this prevents attacks[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Relationship ID prefixing still works** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1134[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1137[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Will still prepend relationship IDs to disambiguate files with same names[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **UUID collision handling still works** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1162[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1167[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Will still add UUIDs for duplicate filenames[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Extension handling still works** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1129[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1132[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Will still add appropriate extensions based on content type[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Additional Considerations[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Same issue in ExtractEmbeddedFiles example**: The example at [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tika-example/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/example/ExtractEmbeddedFiles.java` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m62[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m119[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m has a similar vulnerability and should receive the same fix[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Test Coverage**: The existing tests don't cover path traversal attacks. While [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwe won't modify tests per instructions, the fix should not break existing tests [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msince they only use legitimate file names.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Documentation**: The fix addresses the security concern already documented in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFilenameUtils.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m javadoc[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Harness Code**: The fuzzer harness that triggered this [0m[1;39m([0m[39mTikaAppUnpackerFuzzer[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdoesn't need modification - it's correctly identifying a real vulnerability[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Implementation Details[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix requires modifying approximately [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m30[0m[39m lines in the `[0m[1;35mgetOutputFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod:[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Import Tika's FilenameUtils [0m[1;39m([0m[39mqualify it if needed to avoid conflict[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Replace normalization logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1141[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1154[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add canonical path validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m1160[0m[39m and after line [0m[1;36m1166[0m[1;39m)[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add appropriate error messages for security violations[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix does NOT:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Modify PackageParser [0m[1;39m([0m[39mentry names can remain as-is[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Modify any interfaces or APIs[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Break existing functionality[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Require changes to fuzzing logic[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Modify test code[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
